                                     S 
                                     .

(4) The complementation to the support is a separator.

The assertion follows from the following remark. Let a set  
                               Z 
                             do not intersect the support of an HCF  
                               f 
                            . Then  
                               f 
                               
                                  ( 
                                  Z 
                                  ) 
                               
                               = 
                               0̸ 
                            . Indeed, for every  
                               z 
                               ∈ 
                               Z 
                            ,  
                               f 
                               
                                  ( 
                                  Z 
                                  ) 
                               
                               ∩ 
                               
                                  { 
                                  z 
                                  } 
                               
                               ⊂ 
                               f 
                               
                                  ( 
                                  
                                     { 
                                     z 
                                     } 
                                  
                                  ) 
                               
                               = 
                               0̸ 
                            .

(5) Let  
                               g 
                             be an HCF on  
                               Z 
                             and  
                               f 
                               = 
                               
                                  
                                     j 
                                  
                                  
                                     ∗ 
                                  
                               
                               
                                  ( 
                                  g 
                                  ) 
                               
                            , where  
                               j 
                               : 
                               Z 
                               → 
                               X 
                             is the canonical embedding. Then  
                               Z 
                             is a separator for  
                               f 
                            . Indeed,  
                               
                                  
                                     f 
                                     
                                        ( 
                                        A 
                                        ) 
                                     
                                     = 
                                     g 
                                     
                                        ( 
                                        A 
                                        ∩ 
                                        Z 
                                        ) 
                                     
                                     = 
                                     f 
                                     
                                        ( 
                                        A 
                                        ∩ 
                                        Z 
                                        ) 
                                     
                                     . 
                                  
                               
                             Similarly,  
                               Z 
                             is a separator for the maximal extension  
                               
                                  
                                     j 
                                  
                                  
                                     # 
                                  
                               
                               
                                  ( 
                                  g 
                                  ) 
                               
                            .

(6) If  
                               Z 
                             is a separator for HCFs  
                               f 
                             and  
                               g 
                            , then  
                               Z 
                             is a separator for  
                               f 
                               ∪ 
                               g 
                             and  
                               f 
                               ∩ 
                               g 
                            .

Decomposition and assembly

The set of separators is a topology. This topology reflects a structure of an HCF  
                         f 
                       and allows one to decompose  
                         f 
                       into finer parts (here we assume that  
                         X 
                       is a finite set). Assign to every separator  
                         S 
                       the following CF  
                         
                            
                               f 
                            
                            
                               S 
                            
                         
                       on  
                         S 
                      : for  
                         B 
                         ⊂ 
                         S 
                      ,  
                         
                            
                               
                                  
                                     f 
                                  
                                  
                                     S 
                                  
                               
                               
                                  ( 
                                  B 
                                  ) 
                               
                               = 
                               f 
                               
                                  ( 
                                  B 
                                  ) 
                               
                               ∩ 
                               
                                  
                                     S 
                                  
                                  
                                     ∘ 
                                  
                               
                               . 
                            
                         
                       Obviously, every  
                         
                            
                               f 
                            
                            
                               S 
                            
                         
                       is an HCF, and the following formula of decomposition holds (where  
                         A 
                       is an arbitrary subset of  
                         X 
                      ):

(5) 
                            
                               f 
                               
                                  ( 
                                  A 
                                  ) 
                               
                               = 
                               
                                  
                                     ∐ 
                                  
                                  
                                     S 
                                  
                               
                               
                                  
                                     f 
                                  
                                  
                                     S 
                                  
                               
                               
                                  ( 
                                  A 
                                  ∩ 
                                  S 
                                  ) 
                               
                               . 
                            
                         
                       Indeed,  
                         
                            
                               f 
                            
                            
                               S 
                            
                         
                         
                            ( 
                            A 
                            ∩ 
                            S 
                            ) 
                         
                         = 
                         f 
                         
                            ( 
                            A 
                            ∩ 
                            S 
                            ) 
                         
                         ∩ 
                         
                            
                               S 
                            
                            
                               ∘ 
                            
                         
                         = 
                         
                            ( 
                            f 
                            
                               ( 
                               A 
                               ) 
                            
                            ∩ 
                            S 
                            ) 
                         
                         ∩ 
                         
                            
                               S 
                            
                            
                               ∘ 
                            
                         
                         = 
                         f 
                         
                            ( 
                            A 
                            ) 
                         
                         ∩ 
                         
                            
                               S 
                            
                            
                               ∘ 
                            
                         
                       (in the second equality we use that  
                         S 
                       is a separator for  
                         f 
                      ). Since  
                         X 
                         = 
                         
                            
                               ∐ 
                            
                            
                               S 
                            
                         
                         
                            
                               S 
                            
                            
                               ∘ 
                            
                         
                      , we have  
                         f 
                         
                            ( 
                            A 
                            ) 
                         
                         = 
                         f 
                         
                            ( 
                            A 
                            ) 
                         
                         ∩ 
                         
                            ( 
                            
                               
                                  ∐ 
                               
                               
                                  S 
                               
                            
                            
                               
                                  S 
                               
                               
                                  ∘ 
                               
                            
                            ) 
                         
                         = 
                         
                            
                               ∐ 
                            
                            
                               S 
                            
                         
                         
                            ( 
                            f 
                            
                               ( 
                               A 
                               ) 
                            
                            ∩ 
                            
                               
                                  S 
                               
                               
                                  ∘ 
                               
                            
                            ) 
                         
                         = 
                         
                            
                               ∐ 
                            
                            
                               S 
                            
                         
                         
                            
                               f 
                            
                            
                               S 
                            
                         
                         
                            ( 
                            A 
                            ∩ 
                            S 
                            ) 
                         
                      .

In other words,  
                         f 
                         
                            ( 
                            A 
                            ) 
                         
                       is represented as a disjoint ‘sum’ of smaller pieces  
                         
                            
                               f 
                            
                            
                               S 
                            
                         
                         
                            ( 
                            A 
                            ∩ 
                            S 
                            ) 
                         
                      , and each piece corresponds to its own separator  
                         S 
                      .

Now about a synthesis. Suppose we have a topology on  
                         X 
                       with open sets  
                         S 
                      , and an HCF  
                         
                            
                               f 
                            
                            
                               S 
                            
                         
                       on every  
                         S 
                       which takes values in  
                         
                            
                               S 
                            
                            
                               ∘ 
                            
                         
                      . Then formula  (5)  gives HCF  
                         f 
                       on  
                         X 
                      , and all  
                         S 
                       are its separators.

Here is the simplest particular case:  
                         f 
                       is an HCF on  
                         X 
                       and  
                         Z 
                         ⊂ 
                         X 
                       is a separator for  
                         f 
                      . Then (for  
                         B 
                         ⊂ 
                         Z 
                      )  
                         
                            
                               f 
                            
                            
                               Z 
                            
                         
                         
                            ( 
                            B 
                            ) 
                         
                         = 
                         f 
                         
                            ( 
                            B 
                            ) 
                         
                      , and (for  
                         A 
                         ⊂ 
                         X 
                      )  
                         
                            
                               f 
                            
                            
                               X 
                            
                         
                         
                            ( 
                            A 
                            ) 
                         
                         = 
                         f 
                         
                            ( 
                            A 
                            ) 
                         
                         − 
                         Z 
                      . The decomposition takes the form  
                         
                            
                               f 
                               
                                  ( 
                                  A 
                                  ) 
                               
                               = 
                               f 
                               
                                  ( 
                                  A 
                                  ∩ 
                                  Z 
                                  ) 
                               
                               ∪ 
                               
                                  ( 
                                  f 
                                  
                                     ( 
                                     A 
                                     ) 
                                  
                                  − 
                                  Z 
                                  ) 
                               
                               . 
                            
                         
                       Conversely, suppose we have an HCF  
                         
                            
                               f 
                            
                            
                               Z 
                            
                         
                       on  
                         Z 
                      , an HCF  
                         
                            
                               f 
                            
                            
                               X 
                            
                         
                       on  
                         X 
                      , and  
                         
                            
                               f 
                            
                            
                               X 
                            
                         
                         
                            ( 
                            A 
                            ) 
                         
                       does not intersect  
                         Z 
                       for every  
                         A 
                         ⊂ 
                         X 
                      . Define a choice function  
                         f 
                       by the formula (where  
                         A 
                         ⊂ 
                         X 
                      )  
                         
                            
                               f 
                               
                                  ( 
                                  A 
                                  ) 
                               
                               = 
                               
                                  
                                     f 
                                  
                                  
                                     Z 
                                  
                               
                               
                                  ( 
                                  A 
                                  ∩ 
                                  Z 
                                  ) 
                               
                               ∪ 
                               
                                  
                                     f 
                                  
                                  
                                     X 
                                  
                               
                               
                                  ( 
                                  A 
                                  ) 
                               
                               . 
                            
                         
                       Then  
                         f 
                       is an HCF and  
                         Z 
                       is a separator for  
                         f 
                      .
